\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00335}00335\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ This\ clock\ provides\ the\ current\ time,\ in\ units\ since\ 1970-\/01-\/01}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00336}00336\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ 00:00:00\ UTC\ not\ including\ leap\ seconds.\ \ In\ other\ words,\ UNIX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00337}00337\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ time.\ \ Keep\ in\ mind\ that\ this\ clock\ doesn't\ account\ for\ leap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00338}00338\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ seconds,\ and\ can\ go\ backwards\ (think\ NTP\ adjustments).\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00339}00339\ \ \ \ \ PSNIP\_CLOCK\_TYPE\_WALL\ =\ 1,}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00341}00341\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ process\ is\ active\ (i.e.,\ it\ doesn't\ increment\ while\ blocking\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00342}00342\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ I/O).\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00343}00343\ \ \ \ \ PSNIP\_CLOCK\_TYPE\_CPU\ =\ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00344}00344\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Monotonic\ time\ is\ always\ running\ (unlike\ CPU\ time),\ but\ it\ only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00345}00345\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ ever\ moves\ forward\ unless\ you\ reboot\ the\ system.\ \ Things\ like\ NTP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00346}00346\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ adjustments\ have\ no\ effect\ on\ this\ clock.\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{munit_8c_source_l00347}00347\ \ \ \ \ PSNIP\_CLOCK\_TYPE\_MONOTONIC\ =\ 3}
